DECLARE @inserted27 TABLE ([entryNum] int, [_Position] [int]);
MERGE [ordersTable] USING (
VALUES (@p459, @p460, @p461, @p462, @p463, @p464, @p465, @p466, @p467, @p468, @p469, @p470, @p471, @p472, @p473, @p474, @p475, @p476, @p477, @p478, @p479, @p480, @p481, @p482, @p483, @p484, @p485, @p486, @p487, @p488, @p489, 0),
(@p490, @p491, @p492, @p493, @p494, @p495, @p496, @p497, @p498, @p499, @p500, @p501, @p502, @p503, @p504, @p505, @p506, @p507, @p508, @p509, @p510, @p511, @p512, @p513, @p514, @p515, @p516, @p517, @p518, @p519, @p520, 1)) AS i ([NOFRemarks], [NOFUser], [UPC], [clubID], [collectingEndTime], [collectingStartTime], [created_at], [customerID], [dateProcess], [exception], [item_description], [item_image], [item_price], [item_quantity], [module], [orderId], [order_item_id], [package_number], [platform_status], [pos_price], [runnerStatus], [runnerUser], [shipment_provider], [sku_id], [total_item_price], [tracking_code], [transferLocation], [transferringEndTime], [transferringStartTime], [typeOfexception], [warehouseQuantity], _Position) ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([NOFRemarks], [NOFUser], [UPC], [clubID], [collectingEndTime], [collectingStartTime], [created_at], [customerID], [dateProcess], [exception], [item_description], [item_image], [item_price], [item_quantity], [module], [orderId], [order_item_id], [package_number], [platform_status], [pos_price], [runnerStatus], [runnerUser], [shipment_provider], [sku_id], [total_item_price], [tracking_code], [transferLocation], [transferringEndTime], [transferringStartTime], [typeOfexception], [warehouseQuantity])
VALUES (i.[NOFRemarks], i.[NOFUser], i.[UPC], i.[clubID], i.[collectingEndTime], i.[collectingStartTime], i.[created_at], i.[customerID], i.[dateProcess], i.[exception], i.[item_description], i.[item_image], i.[item_price], i.[item_quantity], i.[module], i.[orderId], i.[order_item_id], i.[package_number], i.[platform_status], i.[pos_price], i.[runnerStatus], i.[runnerUser], i.[shipment_provider], i.[sku_id], i.[total_item_price], i.[tracking_code], i.[transferLocation], i.[transferringEndTime], i.[transferringStartTime], i.[typeOfexception], i.[warehouseQuantity])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[entryNum], i._Position
INTO @inserted27;

SELECT [t].[entryNum] FROM [ordersTable] t
INNER JOIN @inserted27 i ON ([t].[entryNum] = [i].[entryNum])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];
